Complex CSI computation: int8 I/Q → float64 complex → amplitude/phase\n  - RSSI normalization (AGC compensation): `norm = 10^((rssi_ref - rssi)/20)`\n  - Spatial phase unwrapping: correct 2π jumps between adjacent subcarriers\n  - Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n\n- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n  - EMA baseline per link per subcarrier: `baseline = α×amplitude + (1-α)×baseline`\n  - α = dt / (τ + dt) ≈ 0.0033 for dt=0.1s, τ=30s\n  - Motion-gated updates: only update when smoothDeltaRMS < 0.05\n  - Confidence scoring: 0.3 for stale baselines (>7 days), asymptotically → 1.0\n  - Snapshot/restore for SQLite persistence\n  - BaselineManager for multi-link coordination\n\n- **Motion detection (`signal/features.go`):**\n  - NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n\n- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n  - LinkProcessor: ties together phase sanitization, baseline, motion detection\n  - ProcessorManager: manages per-link processors with thread-safe access\n  - GetAllMotionStates(): returns motion state for all links\n  - GetAllBaselines()/RestoreBaseline(): for SQLite persistence\n\n**Constants used (from plan):**\n- RSSIRefdBm = -30.0\n- DefaultMotionThreshold = 0.05\n- DefaultDeltaRMSThreshold = 0.02\n- NBVITopCount = 16\n- NBVIMinThreshold = 0.001\n- DeltaRMSSmoothingAlpha = 0.3\n\n**Tests:** 37 tests covering phase sanitization, baseline, NBVI, motion detection. NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n\n- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n  - LinkProcessor: ties together phase sanitization, baseline, motion detection\n  - ProcessorManager: manages per-link processors with thread-safe access\n  - GetAllMotionStates(): returns motion state for all links\n  - GetAllBaselines()/RestoreBaseline(): for SQLite persistence\n\n**Constants used (from plan):**\n- RSSIRefdBm = -30.0\n- DefaultMotionThreshold = 0.05\n- DefaultDeltaRMSThreshold = 0.02\n- NBVITopCount = 16\n- NBVIMinThreshold = 0.001\n- DeltaRMSSmoothingAlpha = 0.3\n\n**Tests:** 37 tests covering phase sanitization, baseline, NBVI, motion detection. All pass.\n\n**Files created:**\n```\nmothership/internal/signal/\n├── phase.go          — Phase sanitization algorithms\n├── phase_test.go     — 15 tests for phase processing\n├── baseline.go       — EMA baseline management\n├── baseline_test.go  — 9 tests for baseline\n├── features.go       — NBVI selection, deltaRMS, motion detection\n├── features_test.go  — 13 tests for features\n└── processor.go      — LinkProcessor, ProcessorManager\n```\n\n**Remaining for Phase 2:**\n- Dashboard presence indicator\n- CSI recording buffer\n- Adaptive sensing rate\n\n#### Iteration 4 — 2026-03-26\n\n**Completed:** Docker packaging\n\nImplemented container deployment with:\n\n- **Dockerfile:** Multi-stage build for minimal production image\n  - // 2.4 GHz channels: 1-14\n54\t        if (channel <= 14) {\n55\t            return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n56\t        }\n57\t\n58\t        // 5 GHz channels: 36 and above\n59\t        return - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n70\t     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n71\t     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n72\t     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along channel) {\n80\t        // Get wavelength based on channel\n81\t        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n82\t\n83\t        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n84\t        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n85\t\n86\t        // First Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n87\t        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n88\t        const a = (d + lambda / 2) / 2;\n89\t\n90\t        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n91\t        // Using the property that for a prolate spheroid with foci at tx and rx:\n92\t        // b^2 = a^2 - (d/2)^2\n93\t        const b =       };\n114\t    }\n115\t\n116\t    /**\n117\t     * Create a Three.js Mesh for a Fresnel zone ellipsoid.\n118\t     * Creates both wireframe and fill meshes for proper visualization.\n119\t Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n130\t            return null;\n131\t        }\n132\t\n133\t        options = options || {};\n134\t        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n135\t        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n136\t\n137\t        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry\n138\t        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel);\n139\t\n140\t        // Determine segment count based on viewport (mobile optimization)\n141\t        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < CONFIG.mobileViewportWidth;\n142\t        const segments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileSegments : CONFIG.sphereSegments;\n143\t        const heightSegments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileHeightSegments : CONFIG.sphereHeightSegments;\n144\t\n145\t        // Create sphere geometry (unit sphere that will be scaled)\n146\t        const geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(1, segments, heightSegments);\n147\t\n148\t        // Apply non-uniform scaling to create ellipsoid\n149\t        // We scale after creation to get the correct ellipsoid shape\n150\t        geometry.scale(ellipsoid.semiAxes.x, ellipsoid.semiAxes.y, ellipsoid.semiAxes.z);\n151\t\n152\t        // Create wireframe using EdgesGeometry for crisp edges\n153\t        const edgesGeometry = new wireframeOpacity,\n158\t            depthTest: true,\n159\t            depthWrite: false\n160\t        });\n161\t        const wireframe = new THREE.LineSegments(edgesGeometry, true,\n167\t            opacity: fillOpacity,\n168\t            depthWrite: false,\n169\t            side: THREE.DoubleSide\n170\t        });\n171\t        const fill = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, fillMaterial);\n172\t\n173\t        // Position at ellipsoid center\n174\t        wireframe.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n175\t        fill.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n176\t\n177\t        // ellipsoid.lambda,\n187\t            d: ellipsoid.d,\n188\t            a: ellipsoid.a,\n189\t            b: ellipsoid.b,\n190\t            semiAxes: ellipsoid.semiAxes.clone(),\n191\t }\n204\t\n205\t    /**\n206\t     * Add a Fresnel ellipsoid to the scene.\n207\t     * Convenience function that creates and adds the mesh.\n208\t     *\n209\t     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx -   * @param {Object} options - Optional settings\n214\t     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data }\n215\t     */\n216\t    function addFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, removeFresnelEllipsoid(ellipsoid) {\n234\t        if (!ellipsoid) return;\n235\t\n236\t        if (ellipsoid.wireframe && _scene) {\n237\t            _scene.remove(ellipsoid.wireframe);\n238\t * Spaxel Dashboard - Fresnel Zone Helper Module\n *\n * Shared Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry computation for:\n * - Debug overlay (all active links)\n * - Explainability overlay (contributing links for a specific blob)\n *\n * Provides FresnelEllipsoid() function that returns Three.js meshes\n * ready for scene insertion.\n */\n\n(function() {\n    'use strict';\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Configuration\n    // ============================================\n    const CONFIG = {\n        // WiFi wavelengths (c/f in meters)\n        wavelength_5ghz: 0.06,      // 5 GHz\n        wavelength_2_4ghz: 0.125,   // 2.4 GHz\n        // Geometry\n        sphereSegments: 32,         // Sphere geometry segments (reduced on mobile)\n        sphereHeightSegments: 16,\n        wireframeOpacity: 0.6,      // Line opacity for wireframe\n        fillOpacity: 0.08,          // Fill opacity\n        mobileViewportWidth: 768,    // Width threshold for mobile\n        mobileSegments: 16,         // Reduced segments for mobile\n        mobileHeightSegments: 8\n    };\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Private State\n    // ============================================\n    let _scene = null;\n\n    /**\n     * Initialize the Fresnel module with the Three.js scene.\n     * @param {THREE.Scene} scene - The Three.js scene\n     */\n    function init(scene) {\n        _scene = scene;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get WiFi wavelength based on channel number.\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel (1-14 for 2.4 GHz, 36-165 for 5 GHz)\n     * @returns {number} Wavelength in meters\n     */\n    function getWavelengthForChannel(channel) {\n        if (!channel || channel < 1) return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n\n        // 2.4 GHz channels: 1-14\n        if (channel <= 14) {\n            return CONFIG.wavelength_2_4ghz;\n        }\n\n        // 5 GHz channels: 36 and above\n        return CONFIG.wavelength_5ghz;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Calculate Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters for a link.\n     * Based on the first Fresnel zone geometry.\n     *\n     * For a link with TX at position P1 and RX at position P2:\n     * - Link distance d = |P1 - P2|\n     * - WiFi wavelength lambda: 5 GHz -> lambda = 0.06m, 2.4 GHz -> lambda = 0.125m\n     * - Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n     * - Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n     * - Ellipsoid centre: midpoint(P1, P2)\n     * - Ellipsoid orientation: major axis along the P1->P2 unit vector\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number (for wavelength)\n     * @returns {Object} Ellipsoid parameters: { center, semiAxes, rotation, lambda, d, a, b }\n     */\n    function calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel) {\n        // Get wavelength based on channel\n        const lambda = getWavelengthForChannel(channel);\n\n        // Direct distance between TX and RX\n        const d = tx.distanceTo(rx);\n\n        // First Fresnel zone ellipsoid parameters\n        // Semi-major axis: a = (d + lambda/2) / 2\n        const a = (d + lambda / 2) / 2;\n\n        // Semi-minor axis: b = sqrt(a^2 - (d/2)^2)\n        // Using the property that for a prolate spheroid with foci at tx and rx:\n        // b^2 = a^2 - (d/2)^2\n        const b = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, a * a - (d / 2) * (d / 2)));\n\n        // Center of ellipsoid (midpoint between TX and RX)\n        const center = new THREE.Vector3().addVectors(tx, rx).multiplyScalar(0.5);\n\n        // Rotation: align with TX-RX axis\n        // We want the Z-axis of the ellipsoid to point along the link direction\n        const direction = new THREE.Vector3().subVectors(rx, tx).normalize();\n        const up = new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 1); // Z-axis is up in our ellipsoid geometry\n        const quaternion = new THREE.Quaternion().setFromUnitVectors(up, direction);\n\n        return {\n            center: center,\n            semiAxes: new THREE.Vector3(b, b, a), // X, Y (minor), Z (major along link)\n            rotation: quaternion,\n            lambda: lambda,\n            d: d,\n            a: a,\n            b: b,\n            channel: channel\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a Three.js Mesh for a Fresnel zone ellipsoid.\n     * Creates both wireframe and fill meshes for proper visualization.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} color - Color hex value (e.g., 0x4FC3F7 for blue)\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings { wireframeOpacity, fillOpacity }\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data } meshes\n     */\n    function FresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n        if (!_scene) {\n            console.warn('[Fresnel] Scene not initialized. Call Fresnel.init(scene) first.');\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        options = options || {};\n        const wireframeOpacity = options.wireframeOpacity !== undefined ? options.wireframeOpacity : CONFIG.wireframeOpacity;\n        const fillOpacity = options.fillOpacity !== undefined ? options.fillOpacity : CONFIG.fillOpacity;\n\n        // Calculate ellipsoid geometry\n        const ellipsoid = calculateFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel);\n\n        // Determine segment count based on viewport (mobile optimization)\n        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < CONFIG.mobileViewportWidth;\n        const segments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileSegments : CONFIG.sphereSegments;\n        const heightSegments = isMobile ? CONFIG.mobileHeightSegments : CONFIG.sphereHeightSegments;\n\n        // Create sphere geometry (unit sphere that will be scaled)\n        const geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(1, segments, heightSegments);\n\n        // Apply non-uniform scaling to create ellipsoid\n        // We scale after creation to get the correct ellipsoid shape\n        geometry.scale(ellipsoid.semiAxes.x, ellipsoid.semiAxes.y, ellipsoid.semiAxes.z);\n\n        // Create wireframe using EdgesGeometry for crisp edges\n        const edgesGeometry = new THREE.EdgesGeometry(geometry);\n        const wireframeMaterial = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({\n            color: color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: wireframeOpacity,\n            depthTest: true,\n            depthWrite: false\n        });\n        const wireframe = new THREE.LineSegments(edgesGeometry, wireframeMaterial);\n\n        // Create fill mesh\n        const fillMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({\n            color: color,\n            transparent: true,\n            opacity: fillOpacity,\n            depthWrite: false,\n            side: THREE.DoubleSide\n        });\n        const fill = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, fillMaterial);\n\n        // Position at ellipsoid center\n        wireframe.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n        fill.position.copy(ellipsoid.center);\n\n        // Apply rotation to align with link axis\n        wireframe.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n        fill.quaternion.copy(ellipsoid.rotation);\n\n        // Store metadata for raycasting and interactions\n        const data = {\n            tx: tx.clone(),\n            rx: rx.clone(),\n            channel: channel,\n            lambda: ellipsoid.lambda,\n            d: ellipsoid.d,\n            a: ellipsoid.a,\n            b: ellipsoid.b,\n            semiAxes: ellipsoid.semiAxes.clone(),\n            center: ellipsoid.center.clone(),\n            rotation: ellipsoid.rotation.clone()\n        };\n\n        wireframe.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n        fill.userData = { fresnelEllipsoid: data };\n\n        return {\n            wireframe: wireframe,\n            fill: fill,\n            data: data\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a Fresnel ellipsoid to the scene.\n     * Convenience function that creates and adds the mesh.\n     *\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} tx - Transmitter position\n     * @param {THREE.Vector3} rx - Receiver position\n     * @param {number} channel - WiFi channel number\n     * @param {number} color - Color hex value\n     * @param {Object} options - Optional settings\n     * @returns {Object} Object containing { wireframe, fill, data }\n     */\n    function addFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options) {\n        const ellipsoid = FresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, options);\n        if (!ellipsoid) return null;\n\n        if (_scene) {\n            _scene.add(ellipsoid.wireframe);\n            _scene.add(ellipsoid.fill);\n        }\n\n        return ellipsoid;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Remove a Fresnel ellipsoid from the scene.\n     *\n     * @param {Object} ellipsoid - Object returned from addFresnelEllipsoid or FresnelEllipsoid\n     */\n    function removeFresnelEllipsoid(ellipsoid) {\n        if (!ellipsoid) return;\n\n        if (ellipsoid.wireframe && _scene) {\n            _scene.remove(ellipsoid.wireframe);\n            ellipsoid.wireframe.geometry.dispose();\n            if (ellipsoid.wireframe.material) {\n                ellipsoid.wireframe.material.dispose();\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (ellipsoid.fill && _scene) {\n            _scene.remove(ellipsoid.fill);\n            if (ellipsoid.fill.geometry) {\n                ellipsoid.fill.geometry.dispose();\n            }\n            if (ellipsoid.fill.material) {\n                ellipsoid.fill.material.dispose();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ============================================\n    // Public API\n    //       addFresnelEllipsoid: addFresnelEllipsoid,\n        removeFresnelEllipsoid: removeFresnelEllipsoid,\n        // Configuration access\n        CONFIG: CONFIG\n    };\n\n    console.log('[Fresnel] Module loaded');\n})();\n","numLines":270,"startLine":1,"totalLines":270}}},{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_014HfgxKnuSvXuHgjYG7UJFR","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t/**\n2\t     '#84cc16', // zone 2 - lime\n            '#cddc39', // zone 3 - yellow\n            '#ffeb3b', // zone 4 - orange\n            '#ff9800', // zone 5 - deep orange\n        ];\n        return colors[Math.min(zoneNumber - 1, colors.length - 1)] || '#999';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Draw a deltaRMS sparkline on a canvas element.\n     * The right edge represents the detection moment.\n     * A horizontal dashed line shows the motion threshold.\n     *\n     * @param {HTMLCanvasElement} canvas\n     * @param {number[]} points - deltaRMS values over 30 s (oldest first)\n     * @param {number} threshold - motion detection threshold (default 0.02)\n     */\n    function _drawSparkline(canvas, points, threshold) {\n        var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n        var w = canvas.width;\n        var h = canvas.height;\n        threshold = threshold || 0.02;\n\n        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);\n\n        // Background\n        ctx.fillStyle = '#1a1a2e';\n        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);\n\n        var maxVal = threshold * 2;\n        if (points && points.length > 0) {\n            for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n                if (points[i] > maxVal) maxVal = points[i];\n            }\n        }\n        maxVal = maxVal || 0.1;\n\n        // Threshold dashed line\n        var threshY = h - (threshold / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n        ctx.save();\n        ctx.setLineDash([3, 3]);\n        ctx.strokeStyle = '#ff6b6b';\n        ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n        ctx.globalAlpha = 0.7;\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.moveTo(0, threshY);\n        ctx.lineTo(w, threshY);\n        ctx.stroke();\n        ctx.restore();\n\n        if (!points || points.length < 2) {\n            // Single value: draw a flat line at current level\n            var curVal = (points && points.length === 1) ? points[0] : 0;\n            var flatY = h - (curVal / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n            ctx.strokeStyle = '#4FC3F7';\n            ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.moveTo(0, flatY);\n            ctx.lineTo(w - 2, flatY);\n            ctx.stroke();\n        } else {\n            var xStep = (w - 2) / (points.length - 1);\n\n            // Fill area under sparkline\n            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(79, 195, 247, 0.12)';\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n                var x = i * xStep;\n                var y = h - (points[i] / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n                if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, h);\n                ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n            }\n            ctx.lineTo((points.length - 1) * xStep, h);\n            ctx.closePath();\n            ctx.fill();\n\n            // Sparkline\n            ctx.strokeStyle = '#4FC3F7';\n            ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n                var x = i * xStep;\n                var y = h - (points[i] / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n                if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y);\n                else ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n            }\n            ctx.stroke();\n        }\n\n        // Detection marker at right edge\n        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6)';\n        ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.moveTo(w - 1, 0);\n        ctx.lineTo(w - 1, h);\n        ctx.stroke();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Fetch 30-second deltaRMS history for each contributing link and draw sparklines.\n     * Falls back gracefully if the recordings API is unavailable.\n     *\n     * @param {Array} contributingLinks - Array of link contribution objects\n     */\n    function _fetchAndDrawSparklines(contributingLinks) {\n        if (!contributingLinks || contributingLinks.length === 0) return;\n\n        contributingLinks.forEach(function (link) {\n            var safeID = 'sparkline-' + link.link_id.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_');\n            var canvas = document.getElementById(safeID);\n            if (!canvas) return;\n\n            var deltaRMS = link.delta_rms || 0;\n\n            // Try to fetch 30s history from the recordings API\n            fetch('/api/recordings/' + encodeURIComponent(link.link_id) + '/recent?seconds=30')\n                .then(function (resp) {\n                    if (!resp.ok) throw new Error('no data');\n                    return resp.json();\n                })\n                .then(function (data) {\n                    var points = Array.isArray(data.delta_rms) ? data.delta_rms : [deltaRMS];\n                    _drawSparkline(canvas, points, 0.02);\n                })\n                .catch(function () {\n                    // Fallback: render a flat line at the current deltaRMS value\n                    _drawSparkline(canvas, [deltaRMS], 0.02);\n                });\n        });\n    }\n\n    function toggleSection(header) {\n        var content = header.nextElementSibling;\n        var icon = header.querySelector('.toggle-icon');\n        var parentSection = header.parentElement;\n\n        if (content.style.display === 'none') {\n            content.style.display = 'block';\n        // Render Fresnel zone ellipsoids\n        _renderFresnelZones(explanationData);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Save original material states and dim the scene.\n     */\n    function _saveAndDimScene() {\n        _originalMaterialStates.clear();\n\n        // Dim room elements using Viz3D callback\n        if (window.Viz3D.forEachRoomObject) {\n            Viz3D.forEachRoomObject(function(obj) {\n                _dimObject(obj);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Dim all links first (will highlight contributing ones later)\n        if (window.Viz3D.forEachLink) {\n            Viz3D.forEachLink(function(line, linkID) {\n                _dimObject(line);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Dim non-target blobs\n        if (window.Viz3D.forEachBlob) {\n            Viz3D.forEachBlob(function(obj, blobID) {\n                if (blobID !== _currentBlobID && obj.group) {\n                    _dimObject(obj.group);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    function _dimObject(obj) {\n        if (!obj || !obj.material) return;\n\n        var uuid = obj.uuid;\n        if (!uuid) return;\n\n        // Save original state\n        if (!_originalMaterialStates.has(uuid)) {\n            _originalMaterialStates.set(uuid, {\n                opacity: obj.material.opacity,\n                transparent: obj.material.transparent,\n                emissiveIntensity: obj.material.emissiveIntensity || 0\n            });\n            if (obj.material.emissive) {\n obj.material.color.getHex();\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Apply dimming\n        obj.material.opacity = CONFIG.dimOpacity;\n        obj.material.transparent = true;\n        if (obj.material.emissive) {\n            obj.material.emissive.setHex(0x000000);\n            obj.material.emissiveIntensity = 0;\n        }\n        obj.material.needsUpdate = true;\n    }\n\n    /**\n buildSyntheticLinks creates link activations for all node pairs, weighted by\n259\t// how close the target point is to each link's Fresnel zone.\n260\tfunc buildSyntheticLinks(nodes []NodePosition, tx, ty, tz float64) []LinkMotion {\n261\t\tvar links []LinkMotion\n262\t\tfor i := 0; i < len(nodes); i++ {\n263\t\t\tfor j := i + 1; j < len(nodes); j++ {\n264\t\t\t\ta, b := nodes[i], nodes[j]\n265\t\t\t\tdAT := math.Sqrt((tx-a.X)*(tx-a.X) + (ty-a.Y)*(ty-a.Y) + (tz-a.Z)*(tz-a.Z))\n266\t\t\t\tdTB := math.Sqrt((tx-b.X)*(tx-b.X) + (ty-b.Y)*(ty-b.Y) + (tz-b.Z)*(tz-b.Z))\n267\t\t\t\tdAB := math.Sqrt((b.X-a.X)*(b.X-a.X) + (b.Y-a.Y)*(b.Y-a.Y) + (b.Z-a.Z)*(b.Z-a.Z))\n268\t\t\t\texcess := dAT + dTB - dAB\n269\t\n270\t\t\t\tconst lambda = 0.125\n271\t\t\t\tr1 := math.Sqrt(lambda * dAB / 4.0)\n272\t\t\t\tif r1 < 0.1 {\n273\t\t\t\t\tr1 = 0.1\n274\t\t\t\t}\n275\t\t\t\tne := excess / r1\n276\t\t\t\tactivation := 1.0 / (1.0 + ne)\n277\t\t\t\tif activation < 0.05 {\n278\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n279\t\t\t\t}\n280\t\t\t\tlinks = append(links, LinkMotion{\n281\t\t\t\t\tNodeMAC:  a.MAC,\n282\t\t\t\t\tPeerMAC:  b.MAC,\n283\t\t\t\t\tDeltaRMS: activation,\n284\t\t\t\t\tMotion:   true,\n285\t\t\t\t})\n286\t\t\t}\n287\t\t}\n288\t\treturn links\n289\t}\n290\t\n291\t// TestEngine_LastResult checks that LastResult is updated after each Fuse the target point is to each link's Fresnel zone.\nfunc buildSyntheticLinks(nodes []NodePosition, tx, ty, tz float64) []LinkMotion {\n\tvar links []LinkMotion\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(nodes); i++ {\n\t\tfor j := i + 1; j < len(nodes); j++ {\n\t\t\ta, b := nodes[i], nodes[j]\n\t\t\tdAT := math.Sqrt((tx-a.X)*(tx-a.X) + (ty-a.Y)*(ty-a.Y) + (tz-a.Z)*(tz-a.Z))\n\t\t\tdTB := math.Sqrt((tx-b.X)*(tx-b.X) + (ty-b.Y)*(ty-b.Y) + (tz-b.Z)*(tz-b.Z))\n\t\t\tdAB := math.Sqrt((b.X-a.X)*(b.X-a.X) + (b.Y-a.Y)*(b.Y-a.Y) + (b.Z-a.Z)*(b.Z-a.Z))\n\t\t\texcess := dAT + dTB - dAB\n\n\t\t\tconst lambda = 0.125\n\t\t\tr1 := math.Sqrt(lambda * dAB / 4.0)\n\t\t\tif r1 < 0.1 {\n\t\t\t\tr1 = 0.1\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tne := excess / r1\n\t\t\tactivation := 1.0 / (1.0 + ne)\n\t\t\tif activation < 0.05 {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tlinks = append(links, LinkMotion{\n\t\t\t\tNodeMAC:  a.MAC,\n\t\t\t\tPeerMAC:  b.MAC,\n\t\t\t\tDeltaRMS: activation,\n\t\t\t\tMotion:   true,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn links\n}\n\n// TestEngine_LastResult checks that LastResult is updated after each Fuse call.\nfunc TestEngine_LastResult(t *testing.T) {\n\te := makeEngine(10, 3,          []float64 // Normalised [0-1] row-major grid data\n104\t\tRows, Cols             int\n105\t}\n106\t\n107\t// NewHandler creates a new explainability handler.\n108\tfunc NewHandler() *Handler {\n109\t\treturn &Handler{\n110\t\t\tblobHistory:     make(map[int]*BlobExplanation),\n111\t\t\tblobHistoryByTime: make(map[int64]*BlobExplanation),\n112\t\t\tlinkStates:      make(map[string]*LinkState),\n113\t\t\tfusionResult:    &FusionResultSnapshot{},\n114\t\t}\n115\t}\n116\t\n117\t// UpdateBlobs updates the handler with the latest blob and link data.\n118\t// This should be called from the signal processing pipeline whenever blobs are detected.\n119\tfunc (h *Handler) UpdateBlobs(blobs []BlobSnapshot, links []LinkState, grid *GridSnapshot, identity map[int]*BLEMatch) {\n120\t\th.mu.Lock()\n121\t\tdefer h.mu.Unlock()\n122\t\n123\t\t// Update fusion result snapshot\n124\t\th.fusionResult = &FusionResultSnapshot{\n125\t\t\tTimestamp: explanation\n147\t\t}\n148\t\n149\t\t// Clean up old blob history (keep last 100)\n150\t\tif len(h.blobHistory) > 100 {\n151\t\t\t// Remove oldest entries (simple FIFO by recreating map with last 100)\n152\t\t\t// In practice, blob IDs are incrementing, so we can remove IDs < current - 100\n153\t\t\tvar maxID int\n154\t\t\tfor id := range h.blobHistory {\n155\t\t\t\tif id > maxID {\n156\t\t\t\t\tmaxID = id\n157\t\t\t\t}\n158\t\t\t}\n159\t\t\tcutoff := maxID - 100\n160\t\t\tfor id := range h.blobHistory {\n161\t\t\t\tif id < cutoff {\n162\t\t\t\t\tdelete(h.blobHistory, id)\n163\t\t\t\t}\n164\t\t\t}\n165\t\t}\n166\t}\n167\t\n168\t// RegisterRoutes registers the explainability API routes.\n169\tfunc (h *Handler) RegisterRoutes(r chi.Router) ID directly\n224\t\tif explanation, ok := h.blobHistory[blobID]; ok {\n225\t\t\t// Check if the timestamp is close (within 1 minute)\n226\t\t\tif abs64(explanation.Timestamp-timestamp) < 60000 {\n227\t\t\t\twriteJSON(w, explanation)\n228\t\t\t\treturn\n229\t\t\t}\n230\t\t}\n231\t\n232\t\t// If not found by blob ID or timestamp mismatch, search by timestamp\n233\t\t// Find the closest closest)\n247\t\t\treturn\n248\t\t}\n249\t\n250\t\t// Return empty explanation if nothing found\n251\t\texplanation := &BlobExplanation{\n252\t\t\tBlobID:     blobID,\n253\t\t\tX:          0,\n254\t\t\tY:          0,\n255\t\t\tZ:          0,\n256\t\t\tConfidence: 0,\n257\t\t\tTimestamp:  timestamp,\n258\t\t}\n259\t\twriteJSON(w, explanation)\n260\t}\n261\t\n262\t// abs64 returns the absolute value of an int64.\n263\tfunc abs64(x int64) int64 {\n264\t\tif x < 0 {\n265\t\t\treturn -x\n266\t\t}\n267\t\treturn x\n268\t}\n269\t\n270\t// GetExplanationForBlob retrieves the GetExplanationForBlob(blobID int, timestamp int64) *BlobExplanation {\n273\t\th.mu.RLock()\n274\t\tdefer h.mu.RUnlock()\n275\t\n276\t\t// First try to get by blob ID directly\n277\t\tif explanation, explanation\n281\t\t\t}\n282\t\t}\n283\t\n284\t\t// If not found by blob ID or timestamp mismatch, search by timestamp\n285\t\t// Find the closest explanation within 1 minute\n286\t\tvar closest *BlobExplanation\n287\t\tminDiff := int64(60000) // 1 minute\n288\t\n289\t\tfor _, exp := range h.blobHistoryByTime {\n290\t\t\tdiff := abs64(exp.Timestamp - timestamp)\n291\t\t\tif diff < minDiff {\n292\t\t\t\tminDiff = diff\n293\t\t\t\tclosest = exp\n294\t\t\t}\n295\t\t}\n296\t\n297\t\tif closest != nil {\n298\t\t\treturn closest\n299\t\t}\n300\t\n301\t\t// Return nil if nothing found\n302\t\treturn nil\n303\t}\n304\t\n305\t// refreshData handles POST /api/explain/refresh\n306\t// This is called by the dashboard to refresh the explainability data.\n307\tfunc (h *Handler) `json:\"links\"`\n311\t\t\tGridData    *GridSnapshot    `json:\"grid_data,omitempty\"`\n312\t\t\tIdentity    map[int]*BLEMatch `json:\"identity,omitempty\"`\n313\t\t}\n314\t\n315\t\tif err := h.mu.Unlock()\n322\t\n323\t\t// Update fusion result snapshot\n324\t\th.fusionResult = &FusionResultSnapshot{\n325\t\t\tTimestamp: int64(req.GridData.Rows), // placeholder\n326\t\t\tBlobs: len(h.blobHistory),\n347\t\t})\n348\t}\n349\t\n350\t// computeExplanation calculates the explanation for a single blob.\n351\tfunc (h *Handler) computeExplanation(blob BlobSnapshot, links []LinkState, grid *GridSnapshot) *BlobExplanation {\n352\t\tif grid == nil {\n353\t\t\treturn &BlobExplanation{\n354\t\t\t\tBlobID:     blob.ID,\n355\t\t\t\tX:          blob.X,\n356\t\t\t\tY:          blob.Y,\n357\t\t\t\tZ:          blob.Z,\n358\t\t\t\tConfidence: blob.Confidence,\n359\t\t\t\tAllLinks:    []LinkContribution{},\n360\t\t\t}\n361\t\t}\n362\t\n363\t\texplanation := &BlobExplanation{\n364\t\t\tBlobID:            blob.ID,\n365\t\t\tX:                 blob.X,\n366\t\t\tY:                 blob.Y,\n367\t\t\tZ:                 blob.Z,\n368\t\t\tConfidence:        blob.Confidence,\n369\t\t\tContributingLinks: []LinkContribution{},\n370\t\t\tAllLinks:           make([]LinkContribution, 0, len(links)),\n371\t\t\tFresnelZones:      []FresnelZone{},\n372\t\t}\n373\t\n374\t\t// WiFi wavelength constant (2.4 GHz -> ~0.123 m)\n375\t\tconst lambda = 0.123\n376\t\tconst halfLambda = lambda / 2\n377\t\n378\t\t// Compute contribution for each link\n379\t\tfor _, link := range links {\n380\t\t\tlinkID := link.NodeMAC + \":\" + link.PeerMAC\n381\t\n382\t\t\t// Get node positions\n383\t\t\tnodePos := [3]float64{link.NodePos[0], link.NodePos[1], link.NodePos[2]}\n384\t\t\tpeerPos := [3]float64{link.PeerPos[0], link.PeerPos[1], link.PeerPos[2]}\n385\t\n386\t\t\t// Calculate path length excess at blob position\n387\t\t\tpathDirect := math.Sqrt(\n388\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-nodePos[0], 2) +\n389\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-nodePos[1], 2) +\n390\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[2]-nodePos[2], 2))\n391\t\t\tpathViaBlob := math.Sqrt(\n392\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.X-nodePos[0], 2) +\n393\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Y-nodePos[1], 2) +\n394\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Z-nodePos[2], 2)) +\n395\t\t\t\tmath.Sqrt(\n396\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-blob.X, 2) +\n397\t\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-blob.Y, 2) +\n398\t\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[2]-blob.Z, 2))\n399\t\t\tdeltaL := pathViaBlob - pathDirect\n400\t\n401\t\t\t// Fresnel zone number\n402\t\t\tzoneNumber := int(math.Ceil(deltaL / halfLambda))\n403\t\t\tif zoneNumber < 1 {\n404\t\t\t\tzoneNumber = 1\n405\t\t\t}\n406\t\n407\t\t\t// Zone decay function (default decay_rate = 2.0)\n408\t\t\tzoneDecay := 1.0 / math.Pow(float64(zoneNumber), 2.0)\n409\t\n410\t\t\t// Contribution = deltaRMS * weight * zoneDecay\n411\t\t\tcontribution := link.DeltaRMS * link.Weight * zoneDecay\n412\t\n413\t\t\tlinkContrib := LinkContribution{\n414\t\t\t\tLinkID:      linkID,\n415\t\t\t\tNodeMAC:     link.NodeMAC,\n416\t\t\t\tPeerMAC:     link.PeerMAC,\n417\t\t\t\tDeltaRMS:    link.DeltaRMS,\n418\t\t\t\tZoneNumber:  zoneNumber,\n419\t\t\t\tWeight:      link.Weight,\n420\t\t\t\tContributing: link.Motion && link.DeltaRMS > 0.02,\n421\t\t\t\tContribution: contribution,\n422\t\t\t}\n423\t\n424\t\t\texplanation.AllLinks = append(explanation.AllLinks, linkContrib)\n425\t\n426\t\t\tif link.Motion && link.DeltaRMS > 0.02 {\n427\t\t\t\texplanation.ContributingLinks = append(explanation.ContributingLinks, linkContrib)\n428\t\t\t}\n429\t\n430\t\t\t// Add Fresnel zone ellipsoid data for contributing links\n431\t\t\tif link.Motion && link.DeltaRMS > 0.02 {\n432\t\t\t\t// Compute ellipsoid parameters\n433\t\t\t\t// Center is midpoint between nodes\n434\t\t\t\tcenterX := (nodePos[0] + peerPos[0]) / 2\n435\t\t\t\tcenterY := (nodePos[1] + peerPos[1]) / 2\n436\t\t\t\tcenterZ := (nodePos[2] + peerPos[2]) / 2\n437\t\n438\t\t\t\t// Semi-axes approximation for first Fresnel zone\n439\t\t\t\t// The ellipsoid is roughly centered at the midpoint, with the\n440\t\t\t\t// long axis along the link direction\n441\t\t\t\tlinkLength := pathDirect\n442\t\t\t\tlongAxis := linkLength / 2\n443\t\t\t\t// Width of Fresnel zone at this distance\n444\t\t\t\tzoneWidth := 2 * math.Sqrt(math.Pow(lambda*float64(zoneNumber)/2, 2) -\n445\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(float64(zoneNumber-1)*lambda/2, 2))\n446\t\n447\t\t\t\texplanation.FresnelZones = append(explanation.FresnelZones, FresnelZone{\n448\t\t\t\t\tLinkID:     linkID,\n449\t\t\t\t\tCenterPos:  [3]float64{centerX, centerY, centerZ},\n450\t\t\t\t\tSemiAxes:   [3]float64{longAxis, zoneWidth, zoneWidth},\n451\t\t\t\t\tZoneNumber: zoneNumber,\n452\t\t\t\t})\n453\t\t\t}\n454\t\t}\n455\t\n456\t\treturn explanation\n457\t}\n458\t\n459\t// writeJSON writes a JSON response.\n460\tfunc writeJSON(w http.ResponseWriter, v interface{}) {\n461\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n462\t\tdata, err := json.Marshal(v)\n463\t\tif err != nil {\n464\t\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n465\t\t\treturn\n466\t\t}\n467\t\tw.Write(data)\n468\t}\n469\t"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"4dea26b7-f279-4a04-b6f4-3383dd23c61a","uuid":"471d9c90-6900-4b21-8871-2b006a18352e","timestamp":"2026-04-15T14:39:42.563Z","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/home/coding/spaxel/mothership/internal/explainability/handler.go","content":"//       string  `json:\"device_addr\"`\n\tConfidence        float64 `json:\"confidence\"`\n\tMatchMethod       string  `json:\"match_method\"` // \"ble_triangulation\" or \"ble_only\"\n\tReportedByNodes   []string `json:\"reported_by_nodes\"`\n\tTriangulationPos  *[3]float64 `json:\"triangulation_pos,omitempty\"` // [x, y, z]\n}\n\n// FresnelZone describes a Fresnel zone ellipsoid for a link.\ntype FresnelZone struct {\n\tLinkID      string   `json:\"link_id\"`\n\tCenterPos   [3]float64 `json:\"center_pos\"`   // [x, y, z] zone center\n\tSemiAxes    [3]float64 `json:\"semi_axes\"`    // [a, b, c] for ellipsoid\n\tZoneNumber  int      `json:\"zone_number\"`   // zone number for this blob position\n}\n\n// LinkState captures the current state of a link.\ntype LinkState struct {\n\tNodeMAC    string\n\tPeerMAC    string\n\tNodePos    [3]float64 // [x, y, z]\n\tPeerPos    [3]float64 // [x, y, z]\n\tDeltaRMS   float64\n\tMotion     bool\n\tWeight     float64 // Learned weight\n\tHealthScore float64\n}\n\n// FusionResultSnapshot captures the latest fusion result for explainability.\ntype FusionResultSnapshot struct {\n\tTimestamp   int64\n\tBlobs       []BlobSnapshot\n\tGridData    *GridSnapshot\n}\n\n// BlobSnapshot is a lightweight blob representation.\ntype BlobSnapshot struct {\n\tID         int\n\tX, Y, Z    float64\n\tConfidence float64\n\tWeight     float64 // Peak height in the grid\n}\n\n// GridSnapshot captures the fusion grid for computing contributions.\ntype GridSnapshot struct {\n\tWidth, Depth, CellSize float64\n\tOriginX, OriginZ       float64\n\tData                    []float64 // Normalised [0-1] row-major grid data\n\tRows, Cols             int\n}\n\n// NewHandler creates a new explainability handler.\nfunc NewHandler() *Handler {\n\treturn &Handler{\n\t\tblobHistory:     make(map[int]*BlobExplanation),\n\t\tblobHistoryByTime: make(map[int64]*BlobExplanation),\n\t\tlinkStates:      make(map[string]*LinkState),\n\t\tfusionResult:    &FusionResultSnapshot{},\n\t}\n}\n\n// UpdateBlobs updates the handler with the latest blob and link data.\n// This should be called from the signal processing pipeline whenever blobs are detected.\nfunc (h *Handler) UpdateBlobs(blobs []BlobSnapshot, links []LinkState, grid *GridSnapshot, identity map[int]*BLEMatch) {\n\th.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer h.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Update fusion result snapshot\n\th.fusionResult = &FusionResultSnapshot{\n\t\tTimestamp: time.Now().Unix(),\n\t\tBlobs:    blobs,\n\t\tGridData: grid,\n\t}\n\n\t// Update link states\n\tfor _, link := range links {\n\t\tlinkID := link.NodeMAC + \":\" + link.PeerMAC\n\t\th.linkStates[linkID] = &link\n\t}\n\n\t// Generate explanations for each blob\n\tfor _, blob := range blobs {\n\t\texplanation := h.computeExplanation(blob, links, grid)\n\t\tif bleMatch := identity[blob.ID]; bleMatch != nil {\n\t\t\texplanation.BLEMatch = bleMatch\n\t\t}\n\t\th.blobHistory[blob.ID] = explanation\n\t\t// Store by timestamp for feedback lookups\n\t\ttimestamp := time.Now().UnixMilli()\n\t\texplanation.Timestamp = timestamp\n\t\th.blobHistoryByTime[timestamp] = explanation\n\t}\n\n\t// Clean up old blob history (keep last 100)\n\tif len(h.blobHistory) > 100 {\n\t\t// Remove oldest entries (simple FIFO by recreating map with last 100)\n\t\t// In practice, blob IDs are incrementing, so we can remove IDs < current - 100\n\t\tvar maxID int\n\t\tfor id := range h.blobHistory {\n\t\t\tif id > maxID {\n\t\t\t\tmaxID = id\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tcutoff := maxID - 100\n\t\tfor id := range h.blobHistory {\n\t\t\tif id < cutoff {\n\t\t\t\tdelete(h.blobHistory, id)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// RegisterRoutes registers the explainability API routes.\nfunc (h *Handler) RegisterRoutes(r chi.Router) {\n\tr.Get(\"/api/explain/{blobID}\", h.explainBlob)\n\tr.Post(\"/api/explain/refresh\", h.refreshData)\n\tr.Get(\"/api/explain/blob/{blobID}/at/{timestamp}\", h.explainBlobAtTime)\n}\n\n// explainBlob handles GET /api/explain/{blobID}\nfunc (h *Handler) explainBlob(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tblobIDStr := chi.URLParam(r, \"blobID\")\n\tblobID, err := strconv.Atoi(blobIDStr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid blob ID\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\th.mu.RLock()\n\texplanation, ok := h.blobHistory[blobID]\n\th.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif !ok {\n\t\t// Return empty explanation for unknown blob\n\t\texplanation = &BlobExplanation{\n\t\t\tBlobID: blobID,\n\t\t\tX:      0,\n\t\t\tY:      0,\n\t\t\tZ:      0,\n\t\t\tConfidence: 0,\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\twriteJSON(w, explanation)\n}\n\n// explainBlobAtTime handles GET /api/explain/blob/{blobID}/at/{timestamp}\n// Returns the explainability snapshot for a blob at or near a specific timestamp.\n// This is used by the feedback system to explain why a detection occurred.\nfunc (h *Handler) explainBlobAtTime(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tblobIDStr := chi.URLParam(r, \"blobID\")\n\tblobID, err := strconv.Atoi(blobIDStr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid blob ID\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\ttimestampStr := chi.URLParam(r, \"timestamp\")\n\ttimestamp, err := strconv.ParseInt(timestampStr, 10, 64)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid timestamp\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\th.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer h.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// First try to get by blob ID directly\n\tif explanation, ok := h.blobHistory[blobID]; ok {\n\t\t// Check if the timestamp is close (within 1 minute)\n\t\tif abs64(explanation.Timestamp-timestamp) < 60000 {\n\t\t\twriteJSON(w, explanation)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// If not found by blob ID or timestamp mismatch, search by timestamp\n\t// Find the closest explanation within 1 minute\n\tvar closest *BlobExplanation\n\tminDiff := int64(60000) // 1 minute\n\n\tfor _, exp := range h.blobHistoryByTime {\n\t\tdiff := abs64(exp.Timestamp - timestamp)\n\t\tif diff < minDiff {\n\t\t\tminDiff = diff\n\t\t\tclosest = exp\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif closest != nil {\n\t\twriteJSON(w, closest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Return empty explanation if nothing found\n\texplanation := &BlobExplanation{\n\t\tBlobID:     blobID,\n\t\tX:          0,\n\t\tY:          0,\n\t\tZ:          0,\n\t\tConfidence: 0,\n\t\tTimestamp:  timestamp,\n\t}\n\twriteJSON(w, explanation)\n}\n\n// abs64 returns the absolute value of an int64.\nfunc abs64(x int64) int64 {\n\tif x < 0 {\n\t\treturn -x\n\t}\n\treturn x\n}\n\n// GetExplanationForBlob retrieves the explainability snapshot for a blob at or near a specific timestamp.\n// This is a public method used by other handlers (like feedback) to access explainability data.\nfunc (h *Handler) GetExplanationForBlob(blobID int, timestamp int64) *BlobExplanation {\n\th.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer h.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// First try to get by blob ID directly\n\tif explanation, ok := h.blobHistory[blobID]; ok {\n\t\t// Check if the timestamp is close (within 1 minute)\n\t\tif abs64(explanation.Timestamp-timestamp) < 60000 {\n\t\t\treturn int64(60000) // 1 minute\n\n\tfor _, exp := range h.blobHistoryByTime {\n\t\tdiff := abs64(exp.Timestamp - timestamp)\n\t\tif diff < minDiff {\n\t\t\tminDiff = diff\n\t\t\tclosest = exp\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif closest != nil {\n\t\treturn closest\n\t}\n\n\t// Return nil if nothing found\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// refreshData handles POST /api/explain/refresh\n// This is called by the dashboard to refresh the explainability data.\nfunc (h *Handler) refreshData(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tvar req struct {\n\t\tBlobs       []BlobSnapshot    `json:\"blobs\"`\n\t\tLinks       []LinkState      `json:\"links\"`\n\t\tGridData    *GridSnapshot    `json:\"grid_data,omitempty\"`\n\t\tIdentity    map[int]*BLEMatch map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"updated\": len(h.blobHistory),\n\t})\n}\n\n// computeExplanation calculates the explanation for a single blob.\nfunc (h *Handler) computeExplanation(blob BlobSnapshot, links []LinkState, grid *GridSnapshot) *BlobExplanation {\n\tif grid == nil {\n\t\treturn &BlobExplanation{\n\t\t\tBlobID:     blob.ID,\n\t\t\tX:          blob.X,\n\t\t\tY:          blob.Y,\n\t\t\tZ:          blob.Z,\n\t\t\tConfidence: blob.Confidence,\n\t\t\tAllLinks:    []LinkContribution{},\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\texplanation := &BlobExplanation{\n\t\tBlobID:            blob.ID,\n\t\tX:                 blob.X,\n\t\tY:                 blob.Y,\n\t\tZ:                 blob.Z,\n\t\tConfidence:        blob.Confidence,\n\t\tContributingLinks: []LinkContribution{},\n\t\tAllLinks:           make([]LinkContribution, 0, len(links)),\n\t\tFresnelZones:      []FresnelZone{},\n\t}\n\n\t// WiFi wavelength constant (2.4 GHz -> ~0.123 m)\n\tconst lambda = 0.123\n\tconst halfLambda = lambda / 2\n\n\t// Compute contribution for each link\n\tfor _, link := range links {\n\t\tlinkID := link.NodeMAC + \":\" + link.PeerMAC\n\n\t\t// Get node positions\n\t\tnodePos := [3]float64{link.NodePos[0], link.NodePos[1], link.NodePos[2]}\n\t\tpeerPos := [3]float64{link.PeerPos[0], link.PeerPos[1], link.PeerPos[2]}\n\n\t\t// Calculate path length excess at blob position\n\t\tpathDirect := math.Sqrt(\n\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-nodePos[0], 2) +\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-nodePos[1], 2) +\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[2]-nodePos[2], 2))\n\t\tpathViaBlob := math.Sqrt(\n\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.X-nodePos[0], 2) +\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Y-nodePos[1], 2) +\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Z-nodePos[2], 2)) +\n\t\t\tmath.Sqrt(\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-blob.X, 2) +\n\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-blob.Y, 2) +\n\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[2]-blob.Z, 2))\n\t\tdeltaL := pathViaBlob - pathDirect\n\n\t\t// Fresnel zone number\n\t\tzoneNumber := int(math.Ceil(deltaL / halfLambda))\n\t\tif zoneNumber < 1 {\n\t\t\tzoneNumber = 1\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Zone decay function (default decay_rate = 2.0)\n\t\tzoneDecay := 1.0 / math.Pow(float64(zoneNumber), 2.0)\n\n\t\t// Contribution = deltaRMS * weight * zoneDecay\n\t\tcontribution := link.DeltaRMS * link.Weight * zoneDecay\n\n\t\tlinkContrib := LinkContribution{\n\t\t\tLinkID:      linkID,\n\t\t\tNodeMAC:     link.NodeMAC,\n\t\t\tPeerMAC:     link.PeerMAC,\n\t\t\tDeltaRMS:    link.DeltaRMS,\n\t\t\tZoneNumber:  zoneNumber,\n\t\t\tWeight:      link.Weight,\n\t\t\tContributing: link.Motion && link.DeltaRMS > 0.02,\n\t\t\tContribution: contribution,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\texplanation.AllLinks = append(explanation.AllLinks, linkContrib)\n\n\t\tif link.Motion && link.DeltaRMS > 0.02 {\n\t\t\texplanation.ContributingLinks = append(explanation.ContributingLinks, linkContrib)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Add Fresnel zone ellipsoid data for contributing links\n\t\tif link.Motion && link.DeltaRMS > 0.02 {\n\t\t\t// Compute ellipsoid parameters\n\t\t\t// Center is midpoint between nodes\n\t\t\tcenterX := (nodePos[0] + peerPos[0]) / 2\n\t\t\tcenterY := (nodePos[1] + peerPos[1]) / 2\n\t\t\tcenterZ := (nodePos[2] + peerPos[2]) / 2\n\n\t\t\t// Semi-axes approximation for first Fresnel zone\n\t\t\t// The ellipsoid is roughly centered at the midpoint, with the\n\t\t\t// long axis along the link direction\n\t\t\tlinkLength := pathDirect\n\t\t\tlongAxis := linkLength / 2\n\t\t\t// Width of Fresnel zone at this distance\n\t\t\tzoneWidth := 2 * math.Sqrt(math.Pow(lambda*float64(zoneNumber)/2, 2) -\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(float64(zoneNumber-1)*lambda/2, 2))\n\n\t\t\texplanation.FresnelZones = append(explanation.FresnelZones, FresnelZone{\n\t\t\t\tLinkID:     linkID,\n\t\t\t\tCenterPos:  [3]float64{centerX, centerY, centerZ},\n\t\t\t\tSemiAxes:   [3]float64{longAxis, zoneWidth, zoneWidth},\n\t\t\t\tZoneNumber: zoneNumber,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn explanation\n}\n\n// writeJSON writes a JSON response.\nfunc writeJSON(w http.ResponseWriter, v interface{}) {\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\",
